Local News 2

Seventeen-Year-Old Girl 157

Captures a Robber

Old Woman Shouts for Help from Rooftop

Girl's Bravery is Commendable

At around 9:45 PM the night before last, a robbery occurred at the Chen residence near Fangbang Bridge, Minguo Road, French Concession. A seventeen-year-old girl from the Chen household single-handedly captured a robber on the spot, and another was intercepted at the Huacheng Road intersection after being chased. Although it is a minor incident, it is rare in recent society for a weak seventeen-year-old girl to capture a robber. Details are recorded below.

Prosperous Incense in the Buddha Hall: Chen Liansheng, a local resident, 54 years old, lives at No. 568 near Fangbang Bridge, Minguo Road, French Concession. The house is a single-bay shop facing the street. Chen and his family live upstairs. A Buddha hall is set up downstairs to treat all kinds of difficult and complicated diseases. In reality, it is a disguised witch doctor.

The walls of the house are hung with plaques, and the incense is quite prosperous, which has attracted the attention of thieves.

Six Robbers Arrive Suddenly: At 9:45 PM the night before last, after the Chen family had dinner, everyone was resting and preparing to go to bed. Suddenly, six robbers of varying heights and wearing black arrived. Three robbers had guns, and one robber blocked the door as a lookout. Five robbers rushed in together. Chen's seventeen-year-old second daughter, Genbao, was downstairs tidying up chores. A robber pointed a gun and forbade her from making a sound, and then snatched the gold bracelet from Genbao's left arm.

Shouting for Help from the Terrace: At that time, Genbao saw that there were many robbers and that they all had guns, so she had to submit to them. She was driven to the upstairs room with all seven or eight people in the house confined in one room. The robbers then ransacked the chests and cabinets at will. Chen's wife, Zhang, although over forty years old, was naturally alert. Seeing that the robbers were focused on robbing money, she secretly opened the upstairs window and climbed over to the terrace of the neighboring house, shouting for help. A hundred people responded, and immediately the police whistle sounded loudly.

Bravely Knocking Down a Thief: Seeing that things were not going well, the robbers went downstairs together to escape. Just as the last robber rushed down the stairs, Chen's daughter, Genbao, followed closely behind and bravely stepped forward to knock the robber to the ground. The robber could not resist. At the same time, neighbors rushed over, and he surrendered. He was found to have no gun on him. Everyone on the scene was shouting about Genbao's danger. The robber was immediately sent to the detective and taken to the police station.

A Robber is Captured: When the robbers fled, they dispersed to the north and south. Two robbers in black gowns were fleeing north. Detectives in the north had already heard the alarm and rushed to meet them. The two robbers were fleeing to the Hongxiang Pawnshop on Huacheng Road. A detective had already raised his gun and was waiting. One robber stopped and surrendered. A loaded gun was found and taken to the police station. After the detectives interrogated them, they were ordered to be detained separately and sent to the court for strict investigation.

Southeast Xinda Brick Kiln Factory

Workers Surround Police 158

White Fruit Village Robbed and Pillaged

Brick Factory Workers Suspected

Police Investigating Surrounded

Outnumbered, They Were Beaten

At approximately 11 PM the night before last, forty to fifty bandits suddenly appeared in the Dahetou area of Baiguo Village, Tangwan, in the Second District of Shanghai County. They were armed with carrying poles, kitchen knives, iron bars, and flashing flashlights in all directions.

Surrounding the village, they broke into homes and plundered in several directions. The village chief, Kang Ximin, and five other households, including Gong Xuetang, were robbed of silver dollars, clothing, and jewelry worth over a thousand gold pieces. After the bandits had their fill of looting, they carried the stolen goods towards the Xinda Brick Kiln Factory to the southeast and fled. Subsequently, Gong Xuetang, the victim, urgently reported to the local County Public Security Third Branch Police Station and the County Defense Corps Second District, requesting an investigation and arrest. Now, according to villagers from Han Family Wooden Bridge, about half a mile east of the robbed village, on the night in question, they were threshing rice in the fields when they saw people dressed in short clothes,

Resembling Workers, numbering several dozens, all speaking with Shandong Jiangbei accents, passing by towards the kiln factory. After receiving the report, the police station and others investigated and determined that there were no wealthy families in the Dahetou area and that there was no reason for outside bandits to covet the area. It was clearly the work of local people, and the victims also said that they seemed to recognize several of the perpetrators. Therefore, the workers in the kiln factory were highly suspected. The next day, Patrol Officer Wang Jun from the station, along with Gong Xianglin, the deputy commander of the corps, led police officers and corps members to the kiln factory. They first explained the reason to the factory manager, He Peicang, and then

Entered the Factory to Search. Unexpectedly, as soon as the workers saw the sudden appearance of the police officers and corps members, they panicked and became stubbornly defiant. With a shout, all four to five hundred workers in the factory grabbed clubs and

Surrounded and Beaten the Police and Corps Members, and threw bricks and stones indiscriminately. Although the police officers and corps members were all armed with firearms, they were no match for the crowd, and all were beaten and injured. Patrol Officer Wang and the corps commander

Were the Most Seriously Injured, and their breathing was weak. The factory manager, knowing that he had caused a great disturbance, not only comforted the police officers and corps members but also immediately sent Wang and the other person to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. According to the doctors, the injuries of the two were very serious, and there was a risk to their lives. Zhao, the chief of the branch, upon hearing the report, immediately prepared a document and reported it to the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, Director Shen dispatched personnel to the village to investigate the situation in order to

Strictly Apprehend the Stolen Goods and Thieves for Interrogation. He also ordered factory manager He Peicang to hand over the perpetrators to be brought to justice and punished.

Water Police Vigorously Suppress Pirates

Rescuing Male and Female Hostages 159

Capturing Eight Notorious Bandits Alive

The Bandit Leader Shot Dead on the Spot

The Jiangsu Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team's Wusong Fourth District patrol boat recently vigorously suppressed pirates and intercepted two pirate ships off the coast of Hengsha Island, rescuing four hostages, as reported in this newspaper on the 4th. It is now known that one of the two intercepted pirate ships, a three-masted ship, was destroyed when the water police's Pingyang gunboat fired over twenty rapid shots during the fierce battle. The remaining ship was intercepted, and eight pirates were captured alive. The hostages rescued were Ma Yingbin, 48 years old, a doctor from Hupu Baimao; a woman, Ma's wife; an infant, Ma's child; and Ma's nephew, a boy named Gu Shujun, 11 years old. The stolen goods recovered from the pirate ship included

A Large Package of Clothing, a bicycle, a briefcase, two Mauser pistols, one Browning rifle, and ammunition. The names of the captured pirates are as follows: (1) Liu Changyi, 29 years old, Yancheng; (2) Zhou Dingru, 28 years old, Yancheng; (3) Wu Shifan, 24 years old, Funing; (4) Bao Chang, 23 years old, Haizhou; (5) Chen Rongsan, 32 years old, Taixing; (6) Gao San Mazi, 37 years old, Funing; (7) Li Guanhe, 42 years old, Yancheng; (8)

Yang Baofu, 36 years old, Haizhou. The eight pirates above were handed over to the Changshu County Government for interrogation by the water police, as the place of capture was within the Changshu territory. According to the pirates' confession, their leader, named Wei Daye (i.e., Wei Xiucai), was shot dead by the water police during the fierce battle.

Lu Xue's Residence in Western Shanghai

Kidnapping Case Cracked 160

Boy Kidnapped in Yancheng

Transferred and Hidden in Shanghai

You Botang Searched Diligently

Hostage Rescued Only the Day Before

At around 6 PM the day before yesterday, Captain Lu of the Shanghai Special City Public Security Bureau Detective Team dispatched detectives Qi Haitian and Zhang Guangsen to the Sixth District Police Station of Caojiadu in Western Shanghai, where they joined Patrol Officer Wang to

Lead Police Officers and Detective Foreman Liu Shaoxiang to rescue a hostage boy from house number 149 of Lu Xue's residence and arrest two male and female criminals guarding the hostage. The details of the kidnapping and the cracking of the case are as follows:

Boy Kidnapped. You Botang, 26 years old, from Yancheng, Jiangbei, has made a living by farming and is quite frugal, so his family is considered well-off. He has a wife and a son named Da Heshang, who is only six years old and much loved by You. Unexpectedly, at around 9 PM on the twelfth night of the first lunar month this year, two kidnappers suddenly scaled the wall and entered with great force. Without asking any questions, they snatched his son Da Heshang and left. Inquiring about their whereabouts, You was extremely anxious about his kidnapped son. Although he later received several letters from the kidnappers demanding ransom, he was unable to raise the huge sum of money and did not respond. Instead, he inquired about the whereabouts of the kidnappers and the hostage's hiding place until the middle of last month when he

Learned that the boy had been hidden in Shanghai. You then came to Shanghai from his hometown and resided at the home of a friend at number 82, Hengfeng Lane, Dong Wuchang Road, Hongkou, to conduct investigations. On the morning of the day before, he received a report that his son was still hidden at number 149 of Lu Xue's residence on Bailinan Road in Western Shanghai.

Hostage Rescued. After learning this, You reported to Captain Lu of the Special City Public Security Bureau Detective Team, as the place was within the Chinese Concession. Captain Lu immediately dispatched detectives Qi Haitian and Zhang Guangsen, along with the reporter You Botang, to report the situation to the Sixth District Police Station of Caojiadu in Western Shanghai, requesting the dispatch of police to assist in the arrest. District Chief Ren ordered Patrol Officer Wang Yaochen to lead police officers and accompany the personnel to the address, where they indeed found the hostage boy inside. They immediately stepped forward to rescue him and arrested two male and female criminals guarding the hostage. They were taken back to the district, where District Chief Ren interrogated them separately. According to the male criminal, Jia Tongnian, 44 years old, from Yancheng, who worked as a rickshaw puller, the boy was entrusted to him by Zheng Zhusan to watch over and raise, and he was paid fifteen yuan a month. He said that the house was rented through the introduction of Xue San and Xu Shitai. According to the female criminal, Wang, 44 years old, who currently works at the Xinchang Silk Factory, Tongnian is her husband and the boy was entrusted to them by someone; she knows nothing else. After obtaining the confessions, District Chief Ren handed over the two criminals and the hostage to the detectives to be taken back to the team for interrogation.

Continued Detention of Landlords. At around 1 PM yesterday, District Chief Ren believed that the landlord who hid the hostage was quite involved and ordered Detective Foreman Liu Shaoxiang to take detectives Dai Yuanqing, Zhu Fengshan, and Gan Youxin to the house to arrest the two landlords, Cao Xiaoyu, and the people who introduced the rental, Xue San and Xu Shitai. They were taken back to the station, where District Chief Ren interrogated them. According to Cao, 37 years old, from Funing, he has always worked as a handyman. According to Xue, the introducer, 30 years old, from Yancheng, who lives at number 30, Caojiazhai, he works as a telephone craftsman. According to Xu, 33 years old, from Yancheng, he works as a rickshaw puller. The documents were then prepared and submitted to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Young Woman Attempts Suicide in Huangpu River 161

Fortunately, Boat Crew Managed to Rescue Her

She Refuses to Say Why She Was World-Weary

At around 7 AM yesterday morning, a young woman with short hair boarded a ferry at the Dongjiadu Wharf in the South City to cross the Huangpu River. When the boat reached the center of the river, the woman suddenly jumped into the river to commit suicide. Fortunately, the boat crew was quick-witted and immediately managed to rescue her. Upon reaching Pudong, the boat crew handed the woman over to the police on duty, who took her to the Third Branch of the Third District Police Station and transferred her to the Third Branch of the Third District Police Station in Tangqiao Town for interrogation. She claimed to be Shi Xiaodi, 19 years old, a local. She lost her parents at a young age and lives with her brother-in-law, Wang Xinsheng, at number 6, Xinchang Lane, Maoshan Temple, Xiaonanmen, relying on her brother-in-law for support. Wang runs a grain business on Dou Market Street in the South City. She also said that she was not mistreated. When the chief of the station asked her why she was world-weary and committed suicide, she firmly refused to say, only saying that she was suffering from an incurable illness and therefore took this action. The chief of the station then instructed the police officer to borrow a set of dry clothes for her to change into and ordered the police to go to the address and bring Wang Xinsheng to the station to take Shi back.

A Concubine Sues the Principal Wife

Requesting a One-Time Alimony Payment 162

Calculated at a Monthly Rate of 200 Yuan

Demanding 81,600 Yuan

A certain Zhang from Haining was a wealthy merchant in Shanghai who passed away last winter, leaving behind one wife and one concubine. The wife, Shen Yunhe, is 35 years old and lives on Datong Road. She has children. The concubine, Xu Zhuzhen, is 39 years old and has been married to Zhang for ten years without any offspring. After Zhang's death, the principal wife and the concubine could not get along, so the concubine moved to her mother's home at number 637, North Suzhou Road, and hired a lawyer to sue the principal wife, demanding a one-time alimony payment of 81,600 yuan. The calculation method is based on her age of 26 at the time of the lawsuit, assuming a lifespan of 60 years, she still has 34 years to live. Zhang had promised to give her 200 yuan per month, which is 2,400 yuan per year, so for 34 years, she should receive 81,600 yuan. The case had been summoned for hearing twice, with instructions to settle out of court. The defendant, Shen Yunhe, then asked her father, Mr. Shen, to represent her in negotiations with the plaintiff. Xu Zhuzhen, persuaded by relatives, shortened the term to ten years and demanded a lump sum payment of over 26,000 yuan, including the monthly fees owed from before and the litigation costs. However, Shen believed that although she controlled the property left by her husband after his death, she still had children to support. The concubine was only supporting herself, so why would she need this huge sum? Therefore, she did not agree to the concubine's settlement conditions. Thus, the case was returned to the legal path. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Wenrong of the Special District District Court continued the trial. According to the plaintiff, Xu Zhuzhen, her husband, Zhang Zhenyi, had promised to give her 200 yuan per month, and from November of the 17th year to January of the 18th year, she received the full amount. After that, no month was paid in full. According to the defendant, Shen Yunhe, although her husband initially promised to give her 200 yuan per month, he changed it to 100 yuan per month in January of the 18th year, and only two months' worth of fees were not paid since January. From March onwards, she gave 100 yuan per month. The reason why the plaintiff previously demanded 200 yuan per month was that she had secretly taken away the stocks and other securities of the Zhongnan Bank while her husband was ill. After her husband recovered and found out, he hired lawyer Jiang Baoli to send a letter to the bank, stating that and asking the plaintiff to hand them over. She then took the opportunity to make a request. However, the plaintiff is an individual, and her food, clothing, and shelter are all provided for. Her husband therefore reduced the monthly payment to 100 yuan, and I still respected his will and paid it monthly. If she really wants a one-time payment, I can only give her four or five thousand yuan at most. Finally, Zhang's cousin, surnamed Shen, testified in court, saying that he was also present when his cousin promised to give the plaintiff 200 yuan, but he did not know how it was reduced to 100 yuan. Since the two sides had no possibility of reconciliation, Judge Xu ordered the lawyers on both sides to begin their arguments and then ordered a recess for a scheduled pronouncement.

All on Tuesday Evenings

The Shanghai Times reported that on Tuesday, June 3rd,

Someone fired at the French tramway three times in the evening, nearly hitting two passengers on one occasion. The French police are currently investigating the case. Cargo Boats and Rowboats to Exchange for New Licenses 164

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities registers and inspects cargo boats and rowboats and issues licenses with a validity period of one year, from July 1st of each year to June 30th of the following year. The validity period of the licenses issued in the 18th year is about to expire and should be exchanged for new licenses as soon as possible to allow for travel. The bureau has announced the exchange method for boat owners to follow: (1) The exchange period is from July 1st to July 31st. Boat owners should bring their old licenses to the various shipping offices where they originally obtained their licenses to exchange for new licenses. (2) When obtaining a new license, a license fee must be paid. The fee for cargo boats is thirty cents per share, and the fee for rowboats is

twenty cents per share. (3) Boats that have already left the country should wait until they return to the country to exchange for new licenses when they retrieve their licenses. (4) From July onwards, monthly donations must be paid with the new license.

Two Youth from Austria Arrive in Shanghai 165

Touring the World on Motorized Bicycles

The North China Daily News reported that two young university students from Austria, Basa and Sulkowski, touring the world on motorized bicycles, arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the 4th). The two set off from Paris and have traveled through thirty-five countries on four continents. The major cities they have passed through include Marseille, Rome, Madrid, Lisbon, Gibraltar (Europe), Tangier, Algiers, Cairo (North Africa), Jerusalem, Damascus, Ankara (Asia Minor), Constantinople, Sofia, Bucharest, Budapest, Belgrade, Athens (re-entering Eastern Europe), Port Said, Suez (again through North Africa), Sudan, Aden, Mumbai, Kolkata, Colombo (Asia), Melbourne, Sydney (Australia), Penang, Singapore, Yangon, Saigon, Hanoi, Macau, Guangzhou, Hong Kong, and arrived in Shanghai, covering a total of 42,500 li. Most of the journey was on motorized bicycles. They now plan to

Take the car to Nanjing and then return to Shanghai. They originally planned to go to Beiping, but gave up due to the current situation. After that, they will go to Japan and the United States. Initially, there was also a young female artist from Beijing, Ms. Tie Jia Tiena, who accompanied them, and they also brought a police dog. Later, the dog died on the way, and the woman stopped in Palestine due to malaria. Both are engineering students, and the purpose of this trip is to travel to supplement their studies. In the future, they will write a book to record the experiences of this trip.

Detective Team 170

Arrested Fugitives and Robbery Bandits

Wang Shifu, Su Sheng, Lu Xingchun, Wang Yao, Ying Haifa, and Bao Yulin, the leaders of the Zhabei Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, received a secret report from an informant stating that Wu Xiaoshan, Xu Mingxiang, Tang Ruchun, and Cao Si, the bandits who robbed Caojiadu, the side of the Binbei Railway, and the Zhaoshang Lichuan Steamboat on the Suzhou River, were currently hiding in a certain house near the slaughterhouse in Caojiadu. The detectives immediately went to the address to arrest the four men, who were arrested on the spot. Under strict interrogation, Wu confessed that in the fourth month of the lunar calendar, he and Xu Xiao Qizi, Xiao Dexi, and a man surnamed Hu used a gun to rob the Caojia Liu Railway and the Suzhou River Xiaoshu Steamboat. He also confessed to his accomplices Wang Dianzhang, Zhang Shaotang, and Han Xiaolong. The officers arrested Han Xiaolong and others separately at number 18, Hefeng Lane, Roberts Road, number 1, Roberts Road, and along the way on McLean Road in conjunction with the Gordon Road Police. However, Han must be transferred to the team after being jointly interrogated by the Special District Court. All the criminals are currently being held in the team pending further investigation to determine if there are other cases before they are reported to the Judicial Section for investigation.

Zhu Jizhou Recuperating in Shanghai 171

Zhu Jizhou, from Qingpu, is old and sick and has an opium addiction. After being kidnapped at home, the bandits hid the hostage in Pudong. He was later rescued by the Taiping Township Defense Corps of Nanhui County and the Ninth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and a bandit woman was arrested. Zhu is now recuperating in Shanghai for more than ten days and still plans to return to his hometown. It is said that the reward money, compensation, and travel expenses for searching for him cost a total of six or seven thousand yuan. It can be said that it was a misfortune within a misfortune to lose property and save his life.

Someone Provoking the Tianyiwei Mother Factory 172

Demanding Extortion After Renting a House Failed

Carrying Weapons and Attacking the Factory

Workers Rose Up to Respond

Both Sides Were Injured

The manufacturing plant of Tianyiwei Mother Food Company is located at 784 Taopeng Road. The property is owned by Jicheng Silver Company. Tianyi wanted to expand the factory, so they negotiated with the rental office to rent four adjacent houses. Although the lessor had agreed to give them a certain fee, those involved were unwilling. During the Dragon Boat Festival, a man surnamed Zhang went to the Tianyi factory to extort 50 yuan on the pretext, but failed. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at 3 PM, he gathered dozens of people, each armed with ironware, and rushed into the factory to make trouble. However, there were also dozens of workers in the factory, and the two sides were evenly matched, so a fight broke out. As a result, two workers, Ma Fei, were injured on the factory side, and Chen Ruian's head was injured on the other side. The Huishan Police, upon hearing the report, sent detectives to the scene, and they dispersed. Only the injured Chen Ruian was captured and sent to the Special District District Court yesterday morning. Judge Ge summoned Tianyi employee Qian Bingfu and others to explain the process, and Chen confessed that he was passing by and was accidentally beaten. The court ordered the defendant to be detained and the matter reinvestigated at a later date.

Female Beggar Not Bad-Looking 173

Enticed to Be a Wife

Unexpectedly Disowns Her Mother

Qiu Liu, an old woman from Yancheng, carried her seventeen-year-old daughter, Qiu Xiao'er, to Shanghai last winter to escape famine. She begged door to door on Daxing Street outside the West Gate. Qiu Xiao'er was quite good-looking and was favored by Chen Bingnian, a man from Jiangbei. Chen enticed Xiao'er to Caojiadu and forcibly married her as his wife for several months. The mother and daughter met when the woman begged in that area. Unexpectedly, Xiao'er, having had a good time, did not recognize her mother. The woman was very angry and reported to the police, who arrested Chen Bingnian and Qiu Xiao'er and took them to the Sixth District Police Station. They were sent to the District Court for interrogation yesterday.

Wife Having an Affair with Someone, Charged 174

Adulterer Fled Without a Trace

Hong Yuhui, from Hangzhou, married Wang Yafeng as his wife for two years. The woman is now thirty-one years old. After coming to Shanghai from Hangzhou, she was first introduced to the Xian Shi Company Amusement Park as a tea server, but has recently stopped working. Hong, having learned that she had an affair with Liu Shanyong, a man from Ningbo, filed a lawsuit in the Special District District Court. The summons to open

The trial was skipped by Wang, who was in hiding. Only Liu was summoned to the case, ordering the payment of 500 yuan as bail pending trial. Unexpectedly, after Liu was released on bail, he knew that seducing another man's wife was illegal and would be punished by law. As he was going to be handcuffed and imprisoned, he took the opportunity to escape. When the court resumed the trial yesterday morning, Liu had flown away. Only Wang Yafeng was found by Hong and brought back to Shanghai from her original home. She was sent to the Huisi Police Station and transferred to the women's prison. Judge Ge proposed the case for interrogation yesterday, and the woman confessed that because her husband was unemployed and pawned off all her clothes and jewelry, she came to Shanghai and asked Liu to introduce her to a job. There was no ambiguity. Since April 27, she left the amusement park and lived with a girlfriend at Xinkang Lane, Datong Road, for a week before returning to Hangzhou. Her husband had previously received 30 yuan from Liu and promised not to pester her, but now he is suing again. The court ordered the defendant to be detained pending a retrial at a later date.

Economic Pressure Leads to Suicide by Smoke Inhalation 175

Yang Ayu, a local, 29 years old, recently committed suicide by inhaling raw smoke at 1 PM on the fourth afternoon due to economic pressure. She checked into room 19 of the Xinmin Hotel (small inn) at 389 Dong Zilaihuo Street, Edward Road, French Concession, and suddenly had a short-sighted idea. The manager of the hotel, Qian Azhu, learned of this and hired a car to send Yang to Renji Hospital. However, the smoke poison had spread deeply in her abdomen and she died despite medical treatment. The hospital reported to the police, who took the body to the Tongren Fuyuandong mortuary for an autopsy. The details have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the police conducted an investigation and found no family members. The Criminal Division of the French Police reported to Judge Zhu Cheng of the French Public Hall yesterday and confirmed that the deceased had indeed committed suicide by poisoning herself. No relatives were found, so the court ordered photos to be taken and the body to be collected by the hall.

Laundry Shop 176

Trial of the Tragic Death of an Apprentice

The Apprentice Examined, No Wounds Found

Official Orders Defendant to Settle

Last year, Liu Caidong, the 13-year-old son of the widow Liu Mei from Wenzhou, was recommended by a friend to work as an apprentice at the Wanhua Cheng Laundry Shop, owned by Zhang Binghao, a fellow villager, located at No. 2 Jiuxing Lane, Jules Spears Road, in the French Concession. Unexpectedly, in April, while drying clothes in a nearby wasteland with the guest master, Hu Adong from Shaoxing, he was inadvertently kicked in the chest by Hu, resulting in injury. After returning to the shop, the owner was informed and treated him, but he continued to work as usual. However, on the afternoon of the 25th of last month, Liu suddenly died. The shop owner reported to the police, who arrested Hu. The body was sent to the morgue. After an examination by Judge Zhu of the French Concession Court, a Western doctor was ordered to conduct another examination. Yesterday, the police brought Hu to the French Concession Court for questioning. The Western Detective Chief reported that the Western doctor's examination found no injuries on the deceased, suggesting death due to illness. The plaintiff, Liu Mei, the deceased's mother, stated that her husband died early, and she had hoped this son would support her in old age. Now that he has been tragically kicked to death, she seeks justice. When questioned, Hu Adong confessed that he and Liu Caidong went to the wasteland to dry clothes that day. Because Caidong did not secure the rope ends to the wooden stakes, they were blown down by the wind. In a moment of anger, he kicked him, but the deceased continued to work as usual and did not appear injured. He claims he does not know how he died later. He begs for investigation. Judge Zhu ordered Hu to post bail and attempt to settle with the deceased's family. If no settlement is reached, he will be brought back to court for further investigation.

Three More Gambling Dens Busted 177

A French detective discovered that residents Zhang Meiting, Zhu Awu, and Xu Huasheng had privately set up gambling dens using "flower clubs" (a lottery-like gambling game) to lure people to gamble, violating the law. On the previous day, detectives were ordered to search the premises and confiscate flower club documents and silver coins, which were brought to the police station. Yesterday, they were handed over to the French Concession Court for investigation. The three defendants confessed to privately setting up gambling dens to lure people to gamble on flower clubs. Chinese and Western officials sentenced each to a fine of fifty silver dollars as a warning.

Impersonating a Patrol Officer for Extortion 178

A few days ago, a man from Beiping named Gao Liangting went to the Huade Milk and Ice Company on Yidingpan Road in West Shanghai.

Claiming to be a patrol officer at the Sixth District Police Station, he was amiable and

eloquent. He first extorted one yuan from a clerk, Mr. Wei, and then attempted to extort money from the company. The company, suspecting he was an imposter, agreed to pay him five silver dollars on the afternoon of the 5th. Gao believed them and left, thanking them. Later, the company considered the situation and concluded that a patrol officer from the Sixth District would not openly extort money. They suspected an imposter and sent a representative to the Sixth District Police Station to report the matter. Upon receiving the report, Chief Ren of the district was furious that someone dared to impersonate a patrol officer and openly extort money. Yesterday, he dispatched police officers to the company to wait. Around 1 p.m., Gao returned and was immediately arrested and brought back to the station. Chief Ren questioned Gao Yuting, who confessed to being 32 years old from Beiping with no fixed address. He was evasive with further questioning. The case was documented and sent to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau for investigation and punishment.

Jin Kang Pawnshop Pledges to Comply with Stamp Duty Regulations 179

The Zhi Changxiang and four other shops, along with Yuchang Pawnshop, in the Public Concession had previously been summoned by the Special District Court on the 29th of last month for failing to affix stamp duty to invoices and pawn tickets, and were fined according to law. Jin Kang Pawnshop was not present at the initial summons and their case was rescheduled for the 5th of this month. It was previously reported. It has now been learned that the owner of Jin Kang Pawnshop was not in Shanghai at the time of the summons and was therefore unable to attend. On the 3rd of this month, Cheng Side, a representative from the Pawnshop Industry Association, presented a document to the Stamp Duty Bureau stating that the failure to affix stamp duty to the pawn tickets was a temporary error and requested leniency for the first offense. They pledged to purchase and affix stamps in the future. The representative also issued a written guarantee stating that they would accept penalties if they violated the regulations again. The police lawyer has now withdrawn the lawsuit against the pawnshop from the court.

East Ditch Buoy Relocation 189

The Harbour Works Department of the Customs Maritime Affairs Section hereby announces that after investigation, the position of the East Ditch Buoy within the Jianghai Customs jurisdiction will be changed. The details are as follows:

The East Ditch Buoy is scheduled to be relocated around June 20th. No further notice will be given at that time. From the new location, the buoy will be located at South 75 degrees East (according to compass direction) from the Black Point triangulation station, at a distance of 1,900 feet. All hydrographic charts No. 1 and No. 8 published by the Maritime Administration Bureau should be corrected accordingly. This announcement is made for compliance. All ships should pay close attention and record the changes to avoid accidents. May 30th, Republic of China Year 19.

Municipal Health Bureau to Conduct the 5th Registration of Traditional Chinese Medicine Practitioners 190

The Municipal Health Bureau originally scheduled the registration of traditional Chinese medicine practitioners to be held twice a year, in June and December. However, in February of this year, the Ministry of Health issued an order to revise the schedule to once a year in June. The bureau will follow the new regulations starting this year. The 4th registration, which was held in December of last year, has already been completed. The 5th registration is now being held, with the registration period set from the 1st of this month to the end of July.

Letter 192

To the esteemed editor:

Having read your newspaper's local social news section yesterday (the 4th), I found a report entitled "Water Police Painstakingly Suppress Pirates." The details described in the report are not in accordance with the facts. After investigating, it was discovered that the point of departure for all units under our jurisdiction (not just the Xupu Bund patrol boat) in suppressing the bandits was Dongxing Sha, where they engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits for four hours, killing more than ten bandits, capturing eight alive, and rescuing four hostages. A total of three guns were seized, one bandit ship was captured, and one was sunk. A special letter is requested for correction in order to ensure factual accuracy. I respectfully wish the editor of Shen Bao peace. Fourth District of the Jiangsu Water Police Department, June 5th.

Received

Taxing the Import of Silver 193

Xu Peikun

Introduction: Since the sharp decline in silver exchange rates in Shanghai, the impact on the national economy and people's livelihood has been profound and significant. The harm to the economy is worse than floods and fierce beasts. We must plan carefully before it rains and prevent trouble before it happens. Since the beginning, I have suggested ways to prevent silver imports and gambling, aiming for this goal. Subsequently, due to practical obstacles, I variably advocated taxing silver imports, thereby curbing cash exports and gambling, hoping it would be easy to implement quickly and effectively, so that the nation's finances would be stable and the people's economy would be revitalized. Is this not a blessing for the country? This is the first condition that economic researchers should pay attention to in opening the discussion. In other words, the reason for rescuing the financial turmoil is nothing more than seeking to stabilize the nation's finances, make the economy healthier, and enrich the people's lives. It is not like the people of the time argued, analyzing from the exchange rate that there is a need to collect silver taxes, and from the wealth perspective, that there is no need to collect silver taxes. Therefore, we must clearly recognize that the purpose of the tax is to rescue the entire people's economy, not based on a partial reason. The collapse of our nation's economy has reached its extreme. If we always hold the feeling of being far from the high hall, like to exaggerate and use empty words without seeking truth from facts and reversing this tide, then in the tragic disaster of economic suicide, who will be responsible for it? (To be continued)

Green Lawn

Fudan Drama Society Performs Cyrano de Bergerac 195

On the 10th of this month, Liang He (Cyrano de Bergerac), this great play, was finally brought to the Chinese stage by the Fudan Drama Society on the 10th of this month. This is the only unmatched romantic play after Er'na Ni (Hernani) that rekindles the fiery passion of the romantic school in people's hearts. The romanticism that boldly brings the extremely rich poetry to the stage originally satisfied and comforted people for all the things that they could not obtain in the natural world, according to Bacon. He argued that the soul is higher than the real world. The soul needs a greatness, a goodness, a change that cannot be found in nature. Only in the art of the romantic school can these requirements be met. Even now, a group of romantic poets still use Bacon's statement as an excuse. Art is originally an escape from reality. A group of naturalists specialize in imitating nature and expressing all the shortcomings of nature, while romanticists obtain a kind of relief from the natural world. In comparison, this is of course far better.

The romantic movement is continuous as long as the youth of the world still exists, as long as the memory of youth is still preserved, as long as the curious mood still survives, the works of the romantic school will eventually exist.

Rostand's (Cyrano de Bergerac) is an excellent representative typical play of romantic works.

The protagonist Cyrano is a great poet of the seventeenth century and is extremely brave. However, he secretly falls in love with his cousin. However, his cousin Roxane does not pay much attention to him. His nose is so big and ugly that it makes her ignore the passion in his heart. Her heart completely tends to Christian, a simple soul without thought, eloquence, and passion. Cyrano restrains himself extremely. He not only avoids his rival, but he also helps him propose to her, making the two of them combined, and on the battlefield, he protects his rival like a son. Think about it, this is such an embarrassing thing. The person you love is taken away by others, and you still have to do everything possible to fulfill the good deeds of others in order to take care of the happiness of the person you love.

However, after Christian dies, our hero Cyrano still constrains his love for Roxane. He still secretly endures his passion. He does not give any hint at all. Until the very end, when he is about to die, he reveals the words in the last letter written in Christian's name to her. Only then does Roxane know all the details. However, Cyrano always denies that he ever loved her, and dies like that.

The moving part of this play is mostly due to its

unpredictability, the rapid movements, the incredible courage, the sudden arrival of the heroine from a difficult journey to the military camp, Cyrano's impossible restraint for fourteen years after Christian's death - all are as moving as legends and not like those absurd legends. The facts in it are not incredible.

(Cyrano de Bergerac) is not only rich in romantic colors in terms of characters and themes, but also rich in passion in terms of the scenes and poetry. We only need to look at the scene where Cyrano forbids the actor from taking the stage in the theater and duels with the viscount who mocked his nose, and the scene where Cyrano helps his rival propose to Roxane on the moonlit platform, she looks at Christian's beautiful body and listens to Cyrano's moving words - under such a dark night, thinking about it is so seductive.

After Watching (The Merchant of Venice) 196

Mei

The sensational (Merchant of Venice) has now become

a thing of the past. Needless to say, it has left a deep page of glory in the history of the Drama Society's performance, with the same value as (The Second Rosary) once performed by the society. It is also difficult to obliterate in the minds of our audience.

The members of the Drama Society are obviously willing to accept people's criticisms with an open mind. They said this (If you don't see it well, please tell us that the clumsy triers have pointers for improvement). The pointer is indeed not worthy, but I will write down what I saw and felt at the time roughly below.

The artistic performance of all the actors still has considerable skill. Among them, Shen Tongjun's Shylock is the most wonderful. It can be said that he is extremely good. His expression in the scene in the Venetian court is so difficult to perform, but Mr. Shen performed it so meticulously. It is difficult to describe in words. Yu Xiuyun's Portia is not bad, but it is a pity that she speaks too fast, and in many places, she does not have time to express her spirit. It can be said that there are shortcomings in the beauty. As for Huang Yimei's Antonio, he seems to be slightly slow. There are also a few people whose Mandarin is not accurate and pure enough. The Merchant of Venice was originally not easy to perform, especially when it was moved to Shanghai with its exotic atmosphere. Now that there are such achievements, it is really not easy. With the hard work of the society, it is enough to comfort itself.

However, they are willing to accept people's sincere

advice with an open mind, so I will not be polite and say a few sincere words with a sincere attitude.

We will not perform foreign foreign plays, but if we adopt them, of course we hope to move the play from the script to the stage. You must not have the slightest scruples, otherwise you will lose its true color, which is also one of the reasons why we love to watch foreign films but are not satisfied with Chinese films. When Bassanio proposed to Portia and succeeded, how happy was Bassanio! And how willing was Portia! He was so happy that he wanted to hug her photo and shout good things! Beauty, angel! She also said many good things to him!

I am yours, from now on, I will give everything to you. Then she gave him a valuable ring on her hand as a permanent commemoration of their engagement. At this moment, this beautiful moment, this moment so worthy of commemoration, at least there should be a longer sweet kiss and embrace. This is a lifetime affair, and there is no need to discuss it. But they just put it aside indifferently and performed it without even touching their hands. This is such a pity and disappointment to the audience. But why do Ms. Yu and Mr. Chen, who do not love art, want to save this move? As for fearing that people will slander that China is not comparable to foreign countries, there is no need to worry about this. To put it bluntly, artistic people or people who love art will not come to slander. Unless it is that group of ordinary people, what is the criticism they make worthy of consideration? I advise Ms. Yu to release a little courageous spirit. I was a little dissatisfied when I saw it at the time. I thought there should be a hug and a kiss. Later, I went back and looked at the script, and it really should be there.

Also, in terms of makeup, although they are all Western clothes, I feel that it is a bit difficult to be realistic on the female body. The female characters in the play all look like Chinese women wearing Western clothes.

The chest and hips seem to be too flat and should be dressed plumply. In those days, Western girls had two sideburns on both sides of their hair. The author has seen this in many books.

Wouldn't this be too faithful? I don't know if the gentlemen of the Society agree.

The Ice Skating Rink of Fudan University 197

Wei Yin

Because of the hobby of several female students to ice skate, the terrazzo on the Zibin College of Liberal Arts was prohibited by the training director from being used for ice skating. So, speculative students hired workers to build an ice skating rink at the back door of the university. Originally, only a few female students were happy to put on skates and skate on the smooth ground. Now that there is an ice skating rink, male students who are skilled in this way also go to join in the fun.

The ice skating rink of Fudan University opened the day before yesterday. The rink owner's mind is really good. He distributed invitations to all the students of the school on the occasion of the opening. After calculating, there are more than 1,500 students in the coming days. A total of 3,000 copies of invitations and envelopes were spent. This expense is not small.

The business was very good on the first day of opening because the tickets only cost two corners of a small ocean an hour and can be extended. At the same time, several female students who like to ice skate came to participate, and male students generally flocked to them like flies to carrion.

In the center of the ice skating rink, I only saw these butterfly-like female students speeding by. Mischievous male students deliberately blocked their way back and forth. Some even sacrificed their own white Western-style pants, pretending to fall on them and deliberately making things difficult for them. Of course, they did not show weakness either. They would all hold hands together to increase their combat power.

Some students really fell in the center of the ice skating rink, which made everyone laugh. Especially when female students fell, there was a roar of laughter. There was a little girl with two braids who was not very familiar with ice skating and often somersaulted. She always complained to the male students who laughed at her.

The layout of the ice skating rink is very simple, but very plain. Although the light is not very sufficient, the air is still very fresh. I heard that a coffee shop will be opened next to it in the near future. At that time, after ice skating with your lover, holding hands and going to this coffee shop to eat something is not the same as being tired from dancing in the brightly lit and intoxicating dance hall and accompanying your lover to eat something in the Dahua Restaurant.

New Activities of Jinan University Students 198

The Birth of the Green Field Society

Jinan University students attach great importance to extracurricular activities, and there are many various academic groups. However, there is still no perfect organization for art groups. Recently, the birth of a Green Field Society has been able to gather the excellent members of the school to devote themselves to the performance of various literary and artistic activities, such as preparing for public performances and publishing publications, which has created a very strong atmosphere in the school and has almost become the only topic of discussion among students after class. The purpose of this society is to unite young people who love art and promote contemporary art, so the recruitment of members is not limited to the school. Within two weeks of joining the school, there are already more than 30 people. This also shows the great attraction of the society. The society's internal organization temporarily consists of literature, drama, and music departments. The society is scheduled to hold an establishment conference at the Lujia Garden near Jinan University at 1:00 PM this Saturday (June 7). Guests are welcome to visit and there will be various recreational activities for performance. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time. In addition, the society's publication has been named Oasis and will be published before June 15. The drama department of the society is currently preparing to rehearse Shakespeare's masterpiece Julius Caesar and plans to hold its first public performance during the third anniversary of Jinan University.

The Story of World Literature (167) Written by John Macy Translated by Hu Cuchi

Chapter 42 199

Russian Literature of the Nineteenth Century

(War and Peace) is not merely a novel; it is a narrative poem of Russian social life, a history of the Napoleonic Wars era. Its scope is vast, encompassing many short stories. Each person stands before a grand backdrop, moving, and they are truly individual people within that grand drama. The four families who are the protagonists, each person is a character. Tolstoy possesses an unparalleled gift for character depiction. He touches upon a character and makes them come alive. Moreover, he possesses the power of depiction, a sense of the scene, whether it be a panoramic view of the battlefield or the interior of a Moscow home. His story is crowded and extremely complex because there are numerous points of intersecting interests. He instinctively follows a method that, in some places, he calls a principle: never forcing the end of the story but letting it proceed. His (naturalism) is not a theory but a manifestation of his nature, his disposition. He views things correctly and through a non-imaginary lens.

The only flaw of (War and Peace) is that it is too broad; that very breadth renders it amorphous. In (Anna Karenina), the scope is not as vast, and the force is more concentrated. Anna's story moves with the greatest tragic inevitability. Her character and her affairs, like a river flowing toward a waterfall, rush her directly toward her doom. The sinful woman abandons a husband who can be regarded as the complete epitome of cold righteousness for a handsome and vain lover. Thus, she finds herself cut off both from her weary lover and from the society she abandoned. She is punished not by some abstract code of good or evil but by the morality of irreconcilable facts. There is no longer any place for her in life. Thus, suicide is the only solution.

As a contrast to the fervent passion of Anna and her lover is the calm story of Levin and Kitty's family life. This part of the book is only loosely related to the central tragedy. However, because Levin wrestles with the mysteries of existence and sees peace in religious mysticism, it is Tolstoy himself. Tolstoy expounds and explains his own views on ethics, religion, politics, art, and so on, consuming the rest of his life. Turgenev, of whom he said, "In modern European literature, I cannot compare to anyone," believed that Tolstoy's departure from literature was an unforgivable sin. However, one of Tolstoy's unforgivable sins was indulging in mere literature. In this respect, he was a master of the past. In (What is Art?), he sweeps almost all the masterpieces we love, including his own novels, into the rubbish heap. At the age of seventy, he once returned to writing novels, writing (Resurrection). Nevertheless, his motivation was not artistic but practical, to raise money for a persecuted Christian sect, the Doukhobors. Although Tolstoy despised money, he also liked to earn it for others. The book is filled with too many moral purposes, but it also reveals the undiminished power of character depiction and scene realization. The artistic spirit within him takes this opportunity to take revenge. Tolstoy's religious belief, reached through great spiritual labor, is extremely simple, liberated from religious authority and theological sophistry. According to his interpretation, the teachings of Jesus were the Orthodox Church fearing his power, so it expelled him from the Church, and examining his books only increased his power. His religious ideas naturally led him to non-resistance and peaceful anarchism. If he had been poor and nameless, he would have been sent to prison or exiled to Siberia. However, he was a literary king more powerful than earthly kings. If the government had taken harsh measures against him, a wave of protests would have swept across Europe. Therefore, the government shifted the hand of persecution to his humble followers, causing Tolstoy endless sorrow. It was good that he died before 1914.

Tolstoy's major works have been translated into English and are available in inexpensive editions. The best translations are by Aylmer Maude, in several volumes including the most important works, already listed in (The World's Classics series). Maude is the author of (The Life of Tolstoy) in two volumes. In every aspect, even when he rode his beloved pony for too long, the reader finds Tolstoy interesting. His astonishing vitality makes even his most insignificant pages come alive.

Social News

Electrical Enterprises in Japan 200

By Lin Ying-mei

The electrical enterprise was invented in 1882. Five years later, it was introduced to Japan. At that time, in the Meiji 20th year, an electrical plant was established in Tokyo to supply the general needs. It has been over forty years since. Examining its development process, it is roughly the same as in various countries around the world. Initially, it was dedicated to supplying electric lights within the city. Later, with the invention of transformers, the power supply area expanded further than before, extending to the suburbs. Subsequently, electric motors (i.e., motors) were gradually improved, sufficient for industrial power. Thus, they were adopted one after another, and the demand increased sharply. Before long, insulators were invented and improved several times, finally achieving the realization of high-voltage, long-distance power transmission. Major load centers could thus be interconnected. Accordingly, large-scale power plants and high-voltage, long-distance power lines also arose in succession, which is what is known today as the era of super-electricity. Now, the current status of electrical enterprises in Japan is briefly described as follows:

Potential Hydropower for Electricity Generation

According to the survey results at the end of December of Showa 3rd year, the hydropower generation was 2,420,700 kilowatts, and the thermal power generation was 1,420,300 kilowatts, totaling 3,850,000 kilowatts. Hydropower accounted for slightly over 63%, and thermal power accounted for slightly under 37%. According to the survey by the Ministry of Communications, the potential hydropower available for electricity generation in Japan is said to be 14 million horsepower. Judging from the achievements of past development, if assisted by thermal power generation, the total amount of electricity generated can definitely be increased twofold. Due to its geographical conditions, Japan has more rainfall, so it can utilize hydropower for electricity generation. However, the amount of rainfall varies with the seasons, so the most economical method is to use both hydropower and thermal power. The current power generation capacity of thermal power plants is 1,433,000 kilowatts, but usually, only half of it is used, about 718,000 kilowatts, with the rest used to supplement hydropower.

Due to topographical reasons, the locations of hydropower generation in Japan are divided into two major zones: the Japanese Sea coast and the Pacific coast. Thermal power plants with a capacity of 70,000 kilowatts or more are centered around Tokyo, Nagoya, Osaka, and other places, as the location is near the sea, which is convenient for coal transportation. In addition, there are 154,000-volt extra-high-voltage power transmission lines to connect hydropower and thermal power. Japan currently has 2,600 kilometers of 100,000-volt and higher transmission lines and interconnections, and 4,404 kilometers of 50,000-volt and higher lines. As for the highest power transmission pressure, it is currently 154,000 volts. In the future, when transmitting power over even longer distances, it will inevitably increase to 220,000 volts or more.

Distribution of Power Supply

In Showa 2nd year, the total amount of electricity supplied, excluding small power plants with less than 100 kilowatts for business, private use, and official use, was 10,558,880,000 kilowatt-hours. Among them, the Kanto area (centered on Tokyo) accounted for 3,033,000,000, the Chubu area (centered on Nagoya) accounted for 966,900,000, and the Kansai area (centered on Osaka) accounted for 2,639,600,000 kilowatt-hours. The total of the above three major load center areas was 6,639,500,000, which is 63% of the total. Calculating the national average, each person accounts for about 172 kilowatt-hours. According to regional calculations, Kansai is the largest, with each person accounting for about 284 kilowatt-hours, followed by Hokuriku at 228, and Chubu at 206, and Kanto at 200 kilowatt-hours. Further dividing the above three major areas into industrial zones with concentrated populations, the following results are obtained:

Electricity Consumption in Industrial Zones, Showa 2nd Year

| | Population (Millions) | Electricity Consumption (Million kWh) | Average kWh per Person |

| -------------------- | --------------------- | ------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |

| Tokyo Yokohama | 2.037 | 5.478 | 372 |

| Nagoya | 0.605 | 1.428 | 424 |

| Osaka Kobe | 2.305 | 6.189 | 372 |

Electricity for Lighting

At the end of Showa 2nd year, the total number of electricity lighting users was 10,547,235, accounting for 88% of the total number of households in the country. The number of electric lamps was 32,232,991, and the electricity consumption was 736,169 kilowatts, with an average of about 3.1 lamps and 69.7 watts of electricity consumption per household. The reason for the development and prevalence of household electric lights in Japan can be attributed to the following two points: (1) the flat-rate electricity fee system, and (2) the rental system of indoor electric wires and other appliances to favor small users. Among the countries in the world, only Switzerland has a higher level of prevalence than Japan.

As for industrial electricity consumption, at the end of Showa 2nd year, there were 339,741 motors in terms of motive power, with a horsepower of 2,404,644 (1,793,859 kilowatts). The electricity used in the chemical industry other than motive power was 446,326 kilowatts, totaling 2,240,085 kilowatts.

Future Demand for Electricity

Household electric heating has recently become increasingly popular. At the end of Showa 1st year, there were about 106,708 users nationwide, consuming 127,340 kilowatts. In the future, with the improvement of lifestyles, the demand for electric heating will be limitless. Electricity for agricultural use has also shown signs of development in recent years. Observing the situation at the end of Showa 3rd year: in terms of motive power, there were 20,493 motors with a horsepower of 73,965 horsepower; in terms of electric heating, it was 2,857 kilowatts. The total number of lamps for pest control and other agricultural applications was 89,088, with a capacity of 1,661 kilowatts. Electric fans and others were 67 kilowatts, with a total capacity of 59,764 kilowatts. The electricity consumption of electric railways and railway electrification in Showa 1st year was 443,423,000 kilowatt-hours for electric trains (DC) and 131,871,000 kilowatt-hours for railway electrification (AC). If calculated with an annual increase of 90 million kilowatt-hours, the consumption in Showa 3rd year may reach

750 million to 800 million kilowatt-hours.

Electrical Enterprise and Income/Expenditure

At the end of Showa 2nd year, there were a total of 728 electrical enterprises in Japan. Among them, 628 were operated by companies, and 100 were operated by public organizations. Among these 100, only about ten places such as Osaka and Tokyo were operated by prefectures and cities with larger scales. The majority were scattered in remote villages and towns with extremely small scales. It can be seen that most of the electrical enterprises in Japan are in the hands of private individuals. Among the total of 728, 15 have a capital of 50 million yuan or more, and 6 have 100 million yuan or more.

At the end of Showa 2nd year, the total capital was said to be 3,024,200,000 yuan, of which the paid-up capital was 2,677,200,000 yuan, the amount of debt was 888,500,000 yuan, and the loan was 617,500,000 yuan. The total fixed capital was 3,667,400,000 yuan. The total of paid-up capital, debt, and loan was 4,183,200,000 yuan, exceeding the fixed capital by 515,800,000 yuan, most of which was invested by large companies in their affiliated institutions.

The total revenue for the same year was over 763,560,000 yuan, which is equal to 20.8% of the fixed capital. After deducting the total expenditure of 484,020,000 yuan, there was a net profit of 279,560,000 yuan, which is about 10.5% of the paid-up capital.

Recently, various industries in Japan have been vigorously advocating rationalization, and the electrical enterprise cannot be unique. Therefore, it is gradually trending towards large-scale to improve efficiency and unify management. This can enhance capital utilization capacity and promote recruitment. Why not do it?
